<script>
	var CLUETIP_CLOSE = '<img src="images/delete.gif" width="16" height="15"  alt="Close" title="Close"/>';
	var QTIP_LOADING = '<p style="text-align:center;"><img src="images/loader_all_yellow.gif" alt="Loading..."/></p>';
	var masq_need_to_show = false;
	var cluetipInitted = new Array();

	var maskEscHandler = function(e) {
		if (e.which == 27) {
			$('#maskDialog').jqmHide();
		}
	};
	$(document).ready(function() {
		MyASUJS.setDefaults(); //set qtip defaults
		
		$('#maskDialog').jqm({
			trigger: '#maskShow', 
			onShow: function(hash) {
				hash.w.show();
				$(document).bind('keydown', maskEscHandler);
			}, 
			onHide: function(hash) {
				hash.w.hide();
				hash.o.remove();
				$(document).unbind('keydown', maskEscHandler);
			}
		});
		if ($('#maskShow').length > 0 && typeof document.activeElement != "undefined") {
			$(document).keydown(function(e) {
				if (e.which == 86 && document.activeElement.nodeName != "INPUT" && document.activeElement.nodeName != "TEXTAREA") {
					$('#maskDialog').jqmShow();
					e.preventDefault();
				}
			});
		}
		
		if (masq_need_to_show) {
			$('#maskDialog').jqmShow();
		}
		$('.masq-info').cluetip({activation: 'click', width: 200, showTitle: true,
				sticky: true, closePosition: 'title', closeText: CLUETIP_CLOSE,
				arrows: true, local: true });
		$(document).keydown(function(e) {
			if (e.which == 27) {
				$(document).trigger('hideCluetip');
				$(document).trigger('hidepopout');
			}
		});
		// TODO: Do something similar to this for the qTip plugin
		/* add click listener */
		$(document).click(function(e) {
			var c = $("#cluetip:visible");
			if (c.length > 0) {
				if ($("div.ignoreClick", c).length > 0) {
					return;
				}
				var c_pos = c.offset();
				if (e.pageX < c_pos.left || e.pageX > c_pos.left+c.width() ||
					e.pageY < c_pos.top || e.pageY > c_pos.top+c.height() ) {
					// Click outside of cluetip, close it
					$(document).trigger('hideCluetip');
				}
			}
		});

		/* add sparky trigger */
		var k_state = 0, k_array = [38,38,40,40,37,39,37,39,66,65];
		$(document).keydown(function(e) {
			if ( e.keyCode == k_array[k_state] ) {
				k_state++;
			} else {
				k_state = 0;
				return;
			}
			if ( k_state == 10 ) {
				$(document).unbind('keydown',arguments.callee);
				$("#sparky").show();
				k_state = 0;
			}
		});
		
		// add link tracking to all links, now and in the future
		//$("a.tracking").live("click", trackLink); // Deprectated
		$(document).on("click", "a.tracking", trackLink); // Old way that needed attributes 'class' + 'rel' 
		//$("a[data-tracking]").live("click", trackLinkData); // Deprecated
		$(document).on("click", "[data-tracking]", trackLinkData); // Better way that uses dedicated attribute 'data-tracking' 

		
	});
	
	function addLinkTracking() {
		return;
	}
	
	var trackLink = function() {
		trackEvent("Link - student", this.rel);
	};

	var trackLinkData = function() {
		trackEvent("Link - student", $(this).attr('data-tracking'));
	};
	
	function trackEvent(category, description) {
		//console.debug("trackEvent: ["+category+", "+description+"]");
		if (category == null) {
			category = "undefined";
		}
		if (typeof gtag !== "undefined") {
			gtag('event', 'click', {
				'event_category': category,
				'event_label': "/analytics_links/myasu/student/" + description
			});
		}
		return true;
	}
	
	function urlValid(url) {
		var v = new RegExp();
		v.compile("^[A-Za-z]+://[A-Za-z0-9-_]+\\.[A-Za-z0-9-_%&~\?\/.=]+$");
	 	return v.test(url);
	}
	
	function updateUserPref(prefFunc, val, otherData, silentError, callback) {
		

		var token = 'JJf][0VNKUsIoFzk2RedoqqKQrMRErwdTvUcch34wIn5WZqRXZ9yJAIsSWruMiw70vcO9R4r8oY=';
		var ajaxData = { token: token, func: prefFunc, value: val };
		if (typeof otherData != "undefined" && otherData != null) {
			jQuery.extend(ajaxData, otherData);
		}
		var options = {
			cache: false,
			url: "pref",
			type: "POST",
			data: ajaxData 
		};
		if (typeof silentError == "undefined" || !silentError) {
			options['error'] = ajaxUpdateError;
		}
		if (typeof callback == "function") {
			options['success'] = callback;
		}
		$.ajax(options);
	}
	var ajaxUpdateError = function(XMLHttpRequest, textStatus, errorThrown) {
		//if (XMLHttpRequest.status == 403) {
		alert('There was an error updating settings. Please reload page.');
	};

	var AjaxLoaderErrorHandler = function(responseText, textStatus, XMLHttpRequest) {
	    if (textStatus != 'success') {
	    	this.innerHTML = '<i>Error retrieving your information.  Please reload the page to try again.</i><!--\n'+textStatus+'\n-->';
	    }
	};

	/*
	TODO Fix/replace this so that it doesn't assume specific HTML elements 'a', 'img', etc.
	Also, no magic strings built by appending suffixes and no assumption of 'experience'.
	*/
	function myASUToggle(baseID, hash, ajaxUpdate, callback) {
		if (typeof hash == "undefined" || hash == null) {
			hash = "";
		}
		if (typeof ajaxUpdate == "undefined" || ajaxUpdate == null) {
			ajaxUpdate = true;
		}
		
		var showHide;
		
		var $content = $('#'+baseID+'_content');
		var $contentTabs = $('#' + baseID + '_content_tablist');
		if ($content.css('display') != 'none') {
			showHide = 'hide';
			$content.slideUp('fast', callback);
			
			if ($contentTabs.length != 0) {
				$contentTabs.slideUp('fast');
			}
		} else {
			showHide = 'show';
			$content.slideDown('fast', callback);
			
			if ($contentTabs.length != 0) {
				$contentTabs.slideDown('fast');
			}
		}
		
		var $icon = $('#'+baseID+'_toggle img');
		if ($icon.length != 0) {
			var open = 'images/icons/minus.jpg';
			var closed = 'images/icons/plus.jpg';
			
			if ($icon.attr('src') == open) {
				$icon.attr('src', closed);
				$icon.attr('title', 'Open');
				$icon.attr('alt', 'Open');
			} else {
				$icon.attr('src', open);
				$icon.attr('title', 'Close');
				$icon.attr('alt', 'Close');
			}
		}
		
		var $faIcon = $('#'+baseID+'_toggle i');
		if ($faIcon.length != 0) {
			var open = 'fa-minus-circle';
			var closed = 'fa-plus-circle';
			
			if ($faIcon.hasClass(open)) {
				$faIcon.removeClass(open);
				$faIcon.addClass(closed);
				$faIcon.attr('title', 'Open');
			} else {
				$faIcon.removeClass(closed);
				$faIcon.addClass(open);
				$faIcon.attr('title', 'Close');
			}
		}

		var $link = $('#'+baseID+'_toggle a');
		if ($link.length != 0) {
			$link.toggleClass("treeopen");
		}

		if (ajaxUpdate) {
			updateUserPref('changeBoxDisplay', '', {key: 'student_'+baseID, display: showHide, hash: hash}, true);
			trackEvent('Toggle', 'box/'+baseID);
		}
		
		return false;
	}
	
	/*
	A different version of the box toggle function, but still, fix it all, see TODO for the other function.
	*/
	function myASUToggleNoExperience(baseID, hash, ajaxUpdate, callback) {
		if (typeof hash == "undefined" || hash == null) {
			hash = "";
		}
		if (typeof ajaxUpdate == "undefined" || ajaxUpdate == null) {
			ajaxUpdate = true;
		}
		
		var showHide;
		
		var $content = $('#'+baseID+'_content');
		if ($content.css('display') != 'none') {
			showHide = 'hide';
			$content.slideUp('fast', callback);
		} else {
			showHide = 'show';
			$content.slideDown('fast', callback);
		}
		
		var $icon = $('#'+baseID+'_toggle img');
		if ($icon.length != 0) {
			var open = 'images/icons/minus.jpg';
			var closed = 'images/icons/plus.jpg';
			
			if ($icon.attr('src') == open) {
				$icon.attr('src', closed);
				$icon.attr('title', 'Open');
				$icon.attr('alt', 'Open');
			} else {
				$icon.attr('src', open);
				$icon.attr('title', 'Close');
				$icon.attr('alt', 'Close');
			}
		}

		var $icon = $('#'+baseID+'_toggle i');
		if ($icon.length != 0) {
			$icon.toggleClass("fa-plus-circle fa-minus-circle");
		}

		var $link = $('#'+baseID+'_toggle a');
		if ($link.length != 0) {
			$link.toggleClass("treeopen");
		}

		if (ajaxUpdate) {
			updateUserPref('changeBoxDisplay', '', {key: baseID, display: showHide, hash: hash}, true);
			trackEvent('Toggle', 'box/'+baseID);
		}
		
		return false;
	}

	function updateCluetipShaddow() {
		if ($("#cluetip:visible").length > 0) {
			var height = ($("#cluetip-outer").height()+3)+"px";
			$("#cluetip > div").each(function() {
				if (this.id == "") {
					$(this).css("height", height);
				}
			});
		}
	}
	$(document).ready(function() {
		setInterval("updateCluetipShaddow()", 500);
	});

	// Note: if called in view-as mode, will trigger error element
	function handlePinToHomepage(boxToPin, addPin, pinActionElement, saveInProgressElement, saveErrorElement, saveCompleteHideElement) {
		if (saveInProgressElement.is(":visible")) {
			//console.log('handlePinToHomepage already saving! ignoring');
			return;
		}
		pinActionElement.hide();
		saveInProgressElement.show();
		saveErrorElement.hide();

		var ajaxData = {
			token: "JJf][0VNKUsIoFzk2RedoqqKQrMRErwdTvUcch34wIn5WZqRXZ9yJAIsSWruMiw70vcO9R4r8oY=", 
			func: "pin-to-homepage",
			boxToPin: boxToPin,
			addPin: addPin // 1 = add, 0 = remove
		};
		var options = {
			cache: false,
			url: "pref",
			type: "POST",
			data: ajaxData 
		};
		options['error'] = function() {
			//console.log('handlePinToHomepage: error');
			saveInProgressElement.hide();
			saveErrorElement.show();
		};
		options['success'] = function() {
			//console.log('handlePinToHomepage: success');
			saveInProgressElement.hide();
			saveErrorElement.hide();
			saveCompleteHideElement.hide(500);
			saveCompleteHideElement.remove();
		};
		$.ajax(options);
	}

</script>

	<script>
		$(document).ready(function(){			
			$('#site-preferences').cluetip({activation: 'click', attribute:'rel', width: 260, showTitle: true,
				sticky: true, closePosition: 'title', closeText: CLUETIP_CLOSE, arrows: true,
				local: true, onShow: sitePreferencesOnShow
				});
				
			$(document).on("click", "#user-info-popup", function(e) {
				e.preventDefault();
				
				$("#user-info-popup-contents").toggle();
				$("#user-name-angle-up").toggle();
				$("#user-name-angle-down").toggle();
			});
			
			$(document).on("click", "#blog-notification-icon", function(e) {
				e.preventDefault();

				$("#blog-notification-popup-contents").toggle();
				
				if ($("#blog-notification-popup-contents").is(":visible")) {
					setBlogLastViewedTimestamp();
				}
			});
			
			$(document).mouseup(function(e) {
				var container1 = $("#user-info-popup-contents");
				var container2 = $("#user-info-popup");

			    // if the target of the click isn't the container nor a descendant of the container
			    if (!container1.is(e.target) && container1.has(e.target).length === 0
			    		&& !container2.is(e.target) && container2.has(e.target).length === 0) {
			        container1.hide();
					$("#user-name-angle-up").hide();
					$("#user-name-angle-down").show();
			    }
			});
			
			$(document).mouseup(function(e) {
				var container1 = $("#blog-notification-popup-contents");
				var container2 = $("#blog-notification-icon");

			    // if the target of the click isn't the container nor a descendant of the container
			    if (!container1.is(e.target) && container1.has(e.target).length === 0
			    		&& !container2.is(e.target) && container2.has(e.target).length === 0) {
			        container1.hide();
			    }
			});
			
			$.ajax({
		        url: 'myASUBlogFeed',
		        type: 'GET',
		        dataType: "xml"
		    }).done(function(xml) {
				var items = [];
				
				var blogLastViewedTimestamp = $("#blog-last-viewed-timestamp").val();
				var numberOfNewBlogPosts = 0;

				$.each($("item", xml), function(index, element) {
					var dontShowPost = false;

					var dontShowDate = new Date();
					dontShowDate.setDate(dontShowDate.getDate() - 90);

					var pubDate = $(element).find("pubDate").text(); // current pubDate format example: September 15, 2021
					var pubDateTimestamp = new Date(pubDate).getTime();

					if (isNaN(pubDateTimestamp)) {
						pubDate = pubDate.replace(/\s/, 'T');
						pubDateTimestamp = new Date(pubDate).getTime();
					}

					if (dontShowDate > pubDateTimestamp) {
						dontShowPost = true;
					}
					
					if (!dontShowPost) {
						if (blogLastViewedTimestamp != null && blogLastViewedTimestamp != "") {
							var twentyFourHoursAgo = new Date();
							twentyFourHoursAgo.setDate(twentyFourHoursAgo.getDate() - 1);
							
							if (pubDateTimestamp < blogLastViewedTimestamp && pubDateTimestamp < twentyFourHoursAgo.getTime()) {
								dontShowPost = true;
							}
						}
					}
					
					if (!dontShowPost) {
						var title = $(element).find("title").text();
						var description = $(element).find("description").text();
						var url = $(element).find("link").text();
						
						if ((blogLastViewedTimestamp == null || blogLastViewedTimestamp == "") || (blogLastViewedTimestamp != null && blogLastViewedTimestamp != "" && pubDateTimestamp > blogLastViewedTimestamp)) {
							numberOfNewBlogPosts++;
						}
						
						var item = {
							title: title,
							description: description,
							url: url,
							pubDate: pubDate
						};
						
						items.push(item);	
					}
		        });
				
				if (items.length > 0) {
					if (numberOfNewBlogPosts > 0) {
						$("#blog-notification-icon").prop("aria-label", "My ASU Blog Notifications (" + numberOfNewBlogPosts + " New Posts)");
						$("#blog-notification-icon").show();
						$("#blog-notification-badge").html(numberOfNewBlogPosts);
						$("#blog-notification-badge").show();
						$("#blog-notification").prop("title", "My ASU Blog Notifications (" + numberOfNewBlogPosts + " New)");
					} else {
						$("#blog-notification-icon").prop("aria-label", "My ASU Blog Notifications");
						$("#blog-notification-icon").show();
						$("#blog-notification").prop("title", "My ASU Blog Notifications");						
					}
					
					var blogNotificationsTemplate = $("#blog_notifications_tpl").html();
					Mustache.parse(blogNotificationsTemplate);
					$("#blog-notification-popup-contents").html(Mustache.render(blogNotificationsTemplate, {items: items}));
				}
		    }).fail(function(xhr, status, error) {
		    	console.log("There was a problem getting the My ASU blog feed: " + status);
		    });
		});

		var sitePreferencesState = {
			initialView: '',
			staffViewOverride: false,
			pgpDefaultStudent: '',
		};

		function sitePreferencesOnShow(ct, cluetipContext) {
			cluetipContext.find("#header-initial-view-selection").val(sitePreferencesState.initialView);
			cluetipContext.find('#header-staff-view-override').prop('checked', sitePreferencesState.staffViewOverride);
			if ($("#header-pgp-default-student-selection option[value='"+sitePreferencesState.pgpDefaultStudent+"']").length > 0) {
				cluetipContext.find('#header-pgp-default-student-selection').val(sitePreferencesState.pgpDefaultStudent);
			}
		}
		
		function setBlogLastViewedTimestamp() {
			var ajaxData = {
				token: "JJf][0VNKUsIoFzk2RedouZgzYlfLDeupLNd0V3E05oGcVDek[UKl5jfeS[DOXTlvKQ]Ew[5lpE=", 
				func: "set-blog-last-viewed-timestamp"
			};
			var options = {
				cache: false,
				url: "pref",
				type: "POST",
				data: ajaxData 
			};
			options['error'] = function() {
				console.log('An error occurred while trying to update your latest notifications. Please try again or check back later.');
			};
			options['success'] = function() {
				$("#blog-notification").prop("title", "MY ASU Blog Notifications");
				$("#blog-notification-badge").hide();
			};
			$.ajax(options);
		}

	</script>

	
		<script>
			function headerSaveSitePreferences(button) {
				var cluetipContext = $(button).parent().parent(); // only need this hack when the form is in a cluetip popup.
				var savingIndicator = cluetipContext.find('#site-preferences-saving-indicator');
				var savedIndicator = cluetipContext.find('#site-preferences-saved-indicator');
				var errorIndicator = cluetipContext.find('#site-preferences-error-indicator');

				var initialViewSelection = cluetipContext.find('#header-initial-view-selection option:selected').val();
				var staffViewOverride = cluetipContext.find('#header-staff-view-override').is(":checked");
				var pgpDefaultStudent = cluetipContext.find('#header-pgp-default-student-selection option:selected').val();

				if (savingIndicator.is(":visible")) {
					//console.log('already saving! ignoring');
					return false;
				}

				savingIndicator.show();
				savedIndicator.hide();
				errorIndicator.hide();

				var ajaxData = {
					token: "JJf][0VNKUsIoFzk2RedouZgzYlfLDeupLNd0V3E05oGcVDek[UKl5jfeS[DOXTlvKQ]Ew[5lpE=", 
					func: "save-site-preferences",
					initialViewSelection: initialViewSelection,
					staffViewOverride: staffViewOverride,
					pgpDefaultStudent: pgpDefaultStudent
				};

				var options = {
					cache: false,
					url: "pref",
					type: "POST",
					data: ajaxData 
				};
				options['error'] = function() {
					//console.log('headerSaveSitePreferences: error');
					savingIndicator.hide();
					savedIndicator.hide();
					errorIndicator.show();
				};
				options['success'] = function() {
					//console.log('headerSaveSitePreferences: success');
					sitePreferencesState.initialView = initialViewSelection;
					sitePreferencesState.staffViewOverride = staffViewOverride;
					sitePreferencesState.pgpDefaultStudent = pgpDefaultStudent;
					savingIndicator.hide();
					errorIndicator.hide();
					savedIndicator.show();
					setTimeout(function() {
						savedIndicator.hide();
		 				// Try to close the open cluetip with a dom hack
						try {
							$("#cluetip-close").click();
						} catch (ex) {}
					}, 1500);
				};
				$.ajax(options);
			}
		</script>
	



		</div>
	</div>

<script>
var resizeQuicklinkData = null;
var currentViewMoreIds = [];
$(document).ready(function() {
	// load quicklinks
	if ($("#quicklinks-container").length > 0) {
		loadQuicklinks();
	}
	
	$(window).resize(function() {
		if ($("#quicklinks-container").length > 0 && $("#quicklinks-container").is(":visible")) {
			updateQuicklinks(resizeQuicklinkData, false);
		}
	});

	$(document).on('click', '#myasu-main-top .quicklinks-show', function(event) {
		event.preventDefault();

		$('#myasu-main-top .quicklinks-modal-list').toggle();
		$("#myasu-main-top .quicklinks-show [class*='fa-chevron-']").toggleClass("fa-chevron-up fa-chevron-down");
	});

	$(document).on('click', '.shortcuts-box .quicklinks-more', function(event) {
		event.preventDefault();
		
		$("#boxed-quicklinks-show-container").css("height", "auto");

		$('.shortcuts-box .quicklinks-box-more-list').show();
		$('.shortcuts-box .quicklinks-less').show();
		$('.shortcuts-box .quicklinks-more').hide();
	});

	$(document).on('click', '.shortcuts-box .quicklinks-less', function(event) {
		event.preventDefault();
		
		$("#boxed-quicklinks-show-container").css("height", "45px");

		$('.shortcuts-box .quicklinks-box-more-list').hide();
		$('.shortcuts-box .quicklinks-more').show();
		$('.shortcuts-box .quicklinks-less').hide();
	});
	
	$(document).mouseup(function(e) {
		var container1 = $("#myasu-main-top .quicklinks-modal-list");
		var container2 = $("#myasu-main-top .quicklinks-show");

	    // if the target of the click isn't the container nor a descendant of the container
	    if (!container1.is(e.target) && container1.has(e.target).length === 0
	    		&& !container2.is(e.target) && container2.has(e.target).length === 0) {
	        container1.hide();
	        $('#myasu-main-top .quicklinks-modal-list').hide();
        	$("#myasu-main-top .quicklinks-show [class*='fa-chevron-']").removeClass("fa-chevron-up").addClass("fa-chevron-down");
	    }
	});
	
	$(document).on('keydown', function (e) {
		var container = $("#myasu-main-top .quicklinks-modal-list");
		
		if (container.is(":visible") && e.keyCode === 27) {
	  		$("#myasu-main-top .quicklinks-modal-list").hide();
	        	$("#myasu-main-top .quicklinks-show [class*='fa-chevron-']").removeClass("fa-chevron-up").addClass("fa-chevron-down");
		}
	});
	
	$(document).on('click', '.reset-gmail', function() {
		var options = {
			url: "gmail/clearcache",
			type: "POST",
			error: function(response) {
				console.log(response); 
			}
		};
		$.ajax(options);
	});
});

var quicklinksContainerView = {
	"hasTrackingId": function() {
		return this.trackingId != null && this.trackingId != ""
	},
	"isGmailLink": function() {
		return this.id == "gmail"
	},
	"isOpenQuickLinkInNewWin": function() {
		return (this.openNewWin && (this.curated || (!this.curated && !this.isViewAs)) && this.openQuickLinkInNewWin);
	}
};

function loadQuicklinks() {
	$.ajax({
		url: "customizeMyAsu",
		success: function(data) {
			resizeQuicklinkData = data;

			if (data.quicklinksVisibleList != null && data.quicklinksVisibleList != undefined) {
				for (var i = 0; i < data.quicklinksVisibleList.length; i++) {
					data.quicklinksVisibleList[i].openQuickLinkInNewWin = data.openQuickLinkInNewWin;
					data.quicklinksVisibleList[i].isViewAs = data.isViewAs;
				}
			}

			if (data.bookmarksVisible != null && data.bookmarksVisible != undefined) {
				for (var i = 0; i < data.bookmarksVisible.length; i++) {
					data.bookmarksVisible[i].openQuickLinkInNewWin = data.openQuickLinkInNewWin;
					data.bookmarksVisible[i].isViewAs = data.isViewAs;
				}
			}

			if (data.moreBookmarksVisible != null && data.moreBookmarksVisible != undefined) {	
				for (var i = 0; i < data.moreBookmarksVisible.length; i++) {
					data.moreBookmarksVisible[i].openQuickLinkInNewWin = data.openQuickLinkInNewWin;
					data.moreBookmarksVisible[i].isViewAs = data.isViewAs;
				}
			}

			renderQuicklinkContainers(data);

			loadGmailCount();
			startGmailInterval();

			if ($("#quicklinks-container").is(":visible")) {
				determineCutOff(data);
			}
			
			if ($("#show-bookmark-icons-value").val() == "true") {
				populateQuicklinksFavicons($("#quicklinks-container"));
				populateQuicklinksFavicons($("#boxed-quicklinks-container"));
			}
		}
	});
}

function renderQuicklinkContainers(data) {
	var quicklinksContainerTemplate = $("#quicklinks_container_tpl").html();
	Mustache.parse(quicklinksContainerTemplate);
	$("#quicklinks-container").html(Mustache.render(quicklinksContainerTemplate, $.extend(data, quicklinksContainerView)));

	var boxedQuicklinksContainerTemplate = $("#boxed_quicklinks_container_tpl").html();
	Mustache.parse(boxedQuicklinksContainerTemplate);
	$("#boxed-quicklinks-container").html(Mustache.render(boxedQuicklinksContainerTemplate, $.extend(data, quicklinksContainerView)));
}

function updateQuicklinks(data, populateIcons) {
	if (data.quicklinksVisibleList != null && data.quicklinksVisibleList != undefined) {
		for (var i = 0; i < data.quicklinksVisibleList.length; i++) {
			data.quicklinksVisibleList[i].openQuickLinkInNewWin = data.openQuickLinkInNewWin;
			data.quicklinksVisibleList[i].isViewAs = data.isViewAs;
		}
	}

	if (data.bookmarksVisible != null && data.bookmarksVisible != undefined) {
		for (var i = 0; i < data.bookmarksVisible.length; i++) {
			data.bookmarksVisible[i].openQuickLinkInNewWin = data.openQuickLinkInNewWin;
			data.bookmarksVisible[i].isViewAs = data.isViewAs;
		}
	}

	if (data.moreBookmarksVisible != null && data.moreBookmarksVisible != undefined) {	
		for (var i = 0; i < data.moreBookmarksVisible.length; i++) {
			data.moreBookmarksVisible[i].openQuickLinkInNewWin = data.openQuickLinkInNewWin;
			data.moreBookmarksVisible[i].isViewAs = data.isViewAs;
		}
	}

	renderQuicklinkContainers(data);
	
	updateGmailBadge(gmailCount);
	
	determineCutOff(data);
	
	if ($("#show-bookmark-icons-value").val() == "true") {
		if (populateIcons) {
			populateQuicklinksFavicons($("#quicklinks-container"));
		}

		populateQuicklinksFavicons($("#boxed-quicklinks-container"));
	}
}

function determineCutOff(data) {
	var element = document.getElementById("quicklinks-container");
	
	data.moreQuickLinksVisibleList = [];

	var invisibleItems = [];
	var extraFaviconLeft = 0;

	for (var i = 0; i < element.childElementCount; i++) {
		var extraFaviconOffset = 0;
		
		if ($(element.children[i]).find("img").length == 0 && $("#show-bookmark-icons-value").val() == "true") {
			extraFaviconOffset = 20;
		}
		
		if ((element.children[i].offsetLeft + extraFaviconLeft) + (element.children[i].offsetWidth + extraFaviconOffset) > element.offsetLeft + element.offsetWidth) {
			invisibleItems.push(element.children[i]);
			data.moreQuickLinksVisibleList.push(data.quicklinksVisibleList[i]);
		}

		if ($(element.children[i]).find("img").length == 0 && $("#show-bookmark-icons-value").val() == "true") {
			extraFaviconLeft += 20;
		}
	}
	
	if (invisibleItems.length > 1) {
		var quicklinksContainerTemplate = $("#quicklinks_container_more_tpl").html();
		Mustache.parse(quicklinksContainerTemplate);
		$("#has-more-quicklinks").html(Mustache.render(quicklinksContainerTemplate, $.extend(data, quicklinksContainerView)));

		$("#has-more-quicklinks").show();

		for (var i = 0; i < invisibleItems.length; i++) {
			currentViewMoreIds.push($(invisibleItems[i]).find("a").data("id"));
			invisibleItems[i].remove();
		}
	}
}

var gmailInterval = null;
var gmailCount = null;
function startGmailInterval() {
	if (true) {
		gmailInterval = setInterval("loadGmailCount()", 1045000);
	}
};
function stopGmailInterval() {
	if (gmailInterval != null) {
		clearInterval(gmailInterval);
	}
};
function loadGmailCount() {
	var options = {
		url: "gmail/unreadcount",
		type: "GET",
		dataType: 'json',
		success: function(response) {
			updateGmailBadge(response.unreadCount);
		},
		statusCode: {
			403: function() {
				stopGmailInterval();
			}
		},
		error: function(response) {
			console.log(response);
		}
	};
	$.ajax(options);
};

function updateGmailBadge(count) {
	gmailCount = count;

	if (count > 0) {
		$('.gmail-unread-badge').prop('title', count+' Unread Messages');
		$('.gmail-unread-badge .unread-count').text(count);
		$('.gmail-unread-badge').show();

		resizeQuicklinkData.showUnreadCount = true;
	} else {
		$('.gmail-unread-badge').prop('title', count+' Unread Messages');
		$('.gmail-unread-badge').hide();

		resizeQuicklinkData.showUnreadCount = false;
	}

	resizeQuicklinkData.unreadCount = count;

	renderQuicklinkContainers(resizeQuicklinkData);

	determineCutOff(resizeQuicklinkData);
};

</script>

	}

	if (document.getElementById("acad-support-team-box")) {
		$("#acad-support-team-box").load("acadsupportteam?format=ajaxhtml", function() { astBoxInit(); });
	}
	
	
		
		
			
		
	
	
	
});
</script>

<script>
var allTerms = [];
var allTermAbbreviations = {};

$(".student-term-info").each(function() {
	var termCYYT = $(this).data("cyyt").toString();
	var termAbbreviatedDescription = $(this).data("abbreviated-description");
	
	allTerms.push(termCYYT);
	allTermAbbreviations[termCYYT] = termAbbreviatedDescription;
});

var defaultTermTab = '2261';
var sessionStoragePrefix = 'myasuClassesBox-ed538d15caa677a675734870a4667cac94f6e81f';
var userShowGrades = false;
var boxContainerDivName = "classes_content";
var showGradesUserPrefName = "showGrades";
var eventNamePrefix = "myclasses";

var activeBackOnClick; // Stores the onclick for the back button
var activeNextOnClick; // Stores the onclick for the next button
var inactiveOnClick = function() {
	return false;
}
var deactivateBack = true; // Stores if we should disable the button on tab 0
var deactivateNext = true; // Stores if we should disable the button on tab [max]

var gradesShowing = false;
var termNames = [];
var cluetipSchedInitted = [];
var currentTerms = [];

var lmsPopupTippyInstances = [];

function setGrades(newShowing, setAjax) {
	gradesShowing = newShowing;
	$("#"+boxContainerDivName+" .sched .grade").css("display", gradesShowing?"":"none");
	$("#"+boxContainerDivName+" .sched .withdrawn").css("display", gradesShowing?"":"none");
	$("#"+boxContainerDivName+" .gradeDetails").css("display", gradesShowing?"":"none");
	$("#"+boxContainerDivName+" .gradelink").css("display", gradesShowing?"none":"");
	$("#"+boxContainerDivName+" .allclasseswithdrawn").css("display", gradesShowing?"none":"");
	if (setAjax) {
		updateUserPref(showGradesUserPrefName, gradesShowing?"true":"false");
		trackEvent("Toggle", eventNamePrefix+"/"+(gradesShowing?"showGrades":"hideGrades"));
	}
}
function switchToTerm(term, setFocus) {
	// Close a cluetip if there is one open
	$("#cluetip-close").click();
	/* If we have 5 or less terms, skip processing and show */
	if (allTerms.length <= 5) {
		showTerms(allTerms, term, setFocus);
		return;
	}
	var showBefore = 2;
	var showAfter = 2;
	var indexOf = array_indexOf(term, allTerms);
	if (indexOf == -1) {
		//alert("Term not found in index of terms.");
		return;
	}
	if (indexOf < 2) {
		showBefore -= 2-indexOf;
		showAfter += 2-indexOf;
	} else if (indexOf > allTerms.length - 3) {
		showBefore = 4 - ((allTerms.length -1 ) - indexOf);
		showAfter = ((allTerms.length -1 ) - indexOf);
	}
	
	termsToShow = [];
	i = 0;
	beforeCounter = showBefore;
	while (beforeCounter != 0) {
		termsToShow[i++] = allTerms[indexOf-beforeCounter];
		beforeCounter--;
	}
	termsToShow[i++] = allTerms[indexOf];

	var afterCounter = 0;
	while (afterCounter != showAfter) {
		termsToShow[i++] = allTerms[indexOf+afterCounter+1];
		afterCounter++;
	}
	
	showTerms(termsToShow, term, setFocus);
}
	
function showTerms(terms, focusTerm, setFocus) {
	currentTerms = terms;
	$("#myclasses-sched").css("display", "none").empty();
	$("#myclasses-sched_tablist").css("display", "none").empty();
	var defaultTab = 0;
	for(i = 0; i < terms.length; i++) {
		term = terms[i];

		$("#myclasses-sched").append($("#myclasses-holder #classtab-" + term).html());
		$("#myclasses-sched_tablist").append("<button role=\"tab\" aria-selected=\"false\" aria-controls=\"" + term + "_tab\" id=\"classes-link-" + i + "\" data-tab-scope=\"myclasses-sched\" onclick=\"return changedSchedTab(" + i + ");\" tabindex=\"-1\">" + allTermAbbreviations[term] + "</button>");
		if (focusTerm == term) {
			defaultTab = i;
		}
	}
	
	// Add dropdown
	$("#myclasses-sched_tablist").append("<button id=\"myclasses_dropdown\" data-template='myclasses_dropdown_content' class=\"dropdown\" title=\"All Terms\">All Semesters<i class=\"myclasses_dropdown_chevron fas fa-chevron-down\" aria-hidden=\"true\"></i></button>");
	
	$("#myclasses-sched_tablist").css("display", "");
	
	initializeTablist("myclasses-sched");
	
	if (setFocus == null) {
		setFocus = false;
	}
	
	if (terms.length) {
		manualActiveTab(document.getElementById("classes-link-" + defaultTab), setFocus);
		changedSchedTab(defaultTab);

		// init tippy instances
		initMyAsuTippy("#myclasses_dropdown", {placement: "bottom", addLinkTracking: true, arrow: false, offset: [0, 0], disablePadding: true, onShowCallback: function() {
			$("#myclasses_dropdown").removeClass("dropdown-focused");
		}, onHidden: function() {
			$("#myclasses_dropdown").focus();
		}});

		if ($("#in-person-class-popout").length) {
			initMyAsuTippy(".class-remote-classification-in-person-popup", {placement: "right-start"});
		}

		initMyAsuTippy(".class-remote-classification-asu-sync-popup", {placement: "right-start"});

		initMyAsuTippy(".deadline-icon", {placement: "right-start", addLinkTracking: true, ajax: true, showTitle: true, maxWidth: "300px"});

		initMyAsuTippy(".lms-popup", {placement: "right-start", addLinkTracking: true, arrow: false, offset: [0, 0], disablePadding: true});

		initMyAsuTippy(".reg-popup", {placement: "bottom-start", addLinkTracking: true, arrow: false, offset: [0, 0], disablePadding: true});

		initMyAsuTippy(".lms-announce-icon", {placement: "right-start", addLinkTracking: true, ajax: true, disablePadding: true, onShowCallback: function() {
			initTippyMenus(null, "#lms-announce-tippy-content");
		}, onTrigger: function(instance) {
			$(instance.reference).find("i").removeClass("lms-announce-bullhorn-maroon");
			$(instance.reference).find("i").addClass("lms-announce-bullhorn-gray");
		}});

		initMyAsuTippy(".mytranscripts", {placement: "right-start", addLinkTracking: true});

		initMyAsuTippy(".extraTeachers", {placement: "right-start", disablePadding: true});

		initMyAsuTippy(".asr-icon", {placement: "right-start", addLinkTracking: true, ajax: true, disablePadding: true, showTitle: true, onShowCallback: function() {
			initTippyMenus(null, "#asr-tippy-content");
			trackEvent("Popup", "myclasses/asr");
		}, onTrigger: function(instance) {
			$(instance.reference).find("i").removeClass("asr-icon-exclamation-active");
			$(instance.reference).find("i").addClass("asr-icon-exclamation-inactive");
		}});
		// end of init tippy instances
	}

	// Reset cluetips
	cluetipSchedInitted = [];
	
	$("#myclasses-sched").css("display", "block");
	
	addLinkTracking($("#myclasses-sched"));

	$(".lms-error").first().show();
}
function changedSchedTab(idx) {
	saveLastSelectedTab(currentTerms[idx]);
	if (cluetipSchedInitted[idx] == null) {
		cluetipSchedInitted[idx] = 1;

		var relm = $('#myclasses-sched .tab-page:eq('+idx+')');

		$('.myasucourses', relm).cluetip("destroy");
		$('.myasucourses', relm).cluetip({activation: 'click', width: 210, showTitle: false,
			sticky: true, closePosition: 'title', closeText: CLUETIP_CLOSE,
			arrows: true, local: true, onShow: function(ct, c) { 
				addLinkTracking(c);
				$("a:eq(0)", c).focus();
			}});

		$('.zoom-links-popup', relm).cluetip("destroy");
		$('.zoom-links-popup', relm).cluetip({activation: 'click', showTitle: false, 
			sticky: true, closePosition: 'title', closeText: CLUETIP_CLOSE, 
			arrows: true, local: true, onShow: function(ct, c) {  
				addLinkTracking(c); 
				$("a:eq(0)", c).focus(); 
			}});
	}
}

// Helper functions
function array_indexOf(item, arr) {
	for (i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) {
		if (arr[i] == item) {
			return i;
		}
	}
	return -1;
}

function saveLastSelectedTab(term) {
	if (localStorage && sessionStoragePrefix != '') {
		var storage = {
			term: term,
			defaultTermTab: defaultTermTab
		}
		localStorage.setItem(sessionStoragePrefix+"-stu-last-tab", JSON.stringify(storage));
	}
}

function retrieveLastSelectedTab() {
	var ret = 0;
	if (localStorage && sessionStoragePrefix != '') {
		var storage = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(sessionStoragePrefix+"-stu-last-tab"));
		// stored term is only valid as long as the default term is the same as it was when it was stored
		if (storage && storage.defaultTermTab == defaultTermTab && storage.term) {
			ret = storage.term;
		}
	}
	return ret;
}

var courseEvalData = [];
var courseEvalPopupTippyInstances = [];

function processCourseEvalData(evalName, evalCount, linkUrl) {
	//console.log('processing count of ['+evalCount+'] for eval system ['+evalName+'] with url ['+linkUrl+']');

	if (evalCount > 0) {
		// store data from this system
		courseEvalData.push({name: evalName, count: evalCount, linkUrl: linkUrl});

		// update the UI to match the current data for all processed systems
		var totalEvals = 0;
		for (var i = 0; i < courseEvalData.length; i++) {
			totalEvals += courseEvalData[i].count;
		}

		//console.log('found ['+totalEvals+'] total evals across ['+courseEvalData.length+'] systems');

		if (courseEvalData.length == 1) {
			var sysData = courseEvalData[0];
			$('div.course-eval-single-link').show();
			$('a.course-eval-single-link').attr('href', sysData.linkUrl);
			$('span.course-eval-single-link-count').text(sysData.count);
			if (sysData.count > 1) {
				$('span.course-eval-single-link-plural').show();
			}
		} else if (courseEvalData.length > 1) {
			$('div.course-eval-single-link').hide();
			$('div.course-eval-multi-button').show();
			$('span.course-eval-multi-button-count').text(totalEvals);

			var templateLi = $('#course-eval-li-template');
			var listUl = $('#course-eval-ul');
			listUl.empty();
			for (var i = 0; i < courseEvalData.length; i++) {
				var sysData = courseEvalData[i];
				var newLi = templateLi.clone();
				newLi.find('span.course-eval-li-template-link-name').text(sysData.name + (sysData.count > 1 ? 's' : ''));
				newLi.find('span.course-eval-li-template-link-count').text(sysData.count);
				newLi.find('a').attr('href', sysData.linkUrl);
				newLi.appendTo(listUl);
			}

			if (courseEvalPopupTippyInstances == null || courseEvalPopupTippyInstances.length == 0) {
				courseEvalPopupTippyInstances = initMyAsuTippy(".course-eval-popup-btn", {placement: "right-start"});
			} else {
				for (var i = 0; i < courseEvalPopupTippyInstances.length; i++) {
					updateMyAsuTippy(courseEvalPopupTippyInstances[i], {placement: "right-start"});
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

function courseEvalError(system, xhr, status, error) {
	//console.log(system + " course eval xhr error: ["+JSON.stringify(xhr)+"] status=["+status+"], error=["+error+"]");
	var logLevel = "ERROR";
	var logString = system + " course eval error status=["+status+"], error=["+error+"]";
	$.ajax({
		type: "POST",
		url: "telemetry",
		cache: false,
		data: {"function": "log", "logLevel": logLevel, "logString": logString}
	});
}

function initCourseEvals() {
	var univCourseEvalEnabled = $('#univCourseEvalEnabled').val();

	if (univCourseEvalEnabled === 'true') {
		$.ajax({
			url: "?action=getPendingCourseEvaluationCount",
			cache: false,
			timeout: 20000,
			success: function(data) {
				if (data != null) {
					processCourseEvalData('University Evaluation', parseInt(data), '?action=goCoursEval');
				}
			},
			error: function(xhr, status, error) { courseEvalError('univ', xhr, status, error); }
		});
	}
}

$(document).ready(function() {
	if (userShowGrades) {
		setGrades(true, false);
	}
	var lastSelectedTerm = retrieveLastSelectedTab();
	if (lastSelectedTerm != 0 && allTerms.indexOf(lastSelectedTerm) != -1) {
		switchToTerm(lastSelectedTerm);
	} else {
		switchToTerm(defaultTermTab);
	}

	initCourseEvals();

	$("#attend-remotely-banner-dismiss").click(function() {
		$("#attend-remotely-banner").hide();

		var token = $('#my-classes-user-form-token').val();
		if (token !== undefined) {
			var ajaxData = {
				token: token,
				func: "alert-message-dismiss",
				alert: "ATTEND_REMOTELY_BANNER",
				hash: $('#alert-remotely-banner-dismiss-version-hash').val(),
			};

			$.ajax({
				cache: false,
				url: "pref",
				type: "POST",
				data: ajaxData,
				error: function() {
					//console.log('Error storing system message dismissal!');
				}
			});
		}
	});

	$("#attend-remotely-banner-dismiss-2").click(function() {
		$("#attend-remotely-banner-2").hide();

		var token = $('#global-user-form-token').val();
		if (token !== undefined) {
			var ajaxData = {
				token: token,
				func: "alert-message-dismiss",
				alert: "ATTEND_REMOTELY_BANNER2",
				hash: $('#alert-remotely-banner-dismiss-version-hash-2').val(),
			};

			$.ajax({
				cache: false,
				url: "pref",
				type: "POST",
				data: ajaxData,
				error: function() {
					//console.log('Error storing system message dismissal!');
				}
			});
		}
	});
	
	$(".my-classes-empty-state-container").on("click", "#download-session-to-calendar", function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
		var tempLink = document.createElement("a");
		tempLink.download = "Course_Planning_Session.ics";
		tempLink.href = "classAdvisingSession";

		document.body.appendChild(tempLink);

		tempLink.click();

		document.body.removeChild(tempLink);

		delete tempLink;
	});
});

<script>
	$(document).ready(function() {
		var degreeSearchBaseUrl = $("#degree-search-base-url").val();

		$("#search-undergraduate-degrees").on("click", function() {
			var keyword = $("#undergraduate-degrees-search").val();
			if (degreeSearchBaseUrl && keyword) {
				document.location.href = degreeSearchBaseUrl + "/bachelors/major-list/keyword/" + encodeURIComponent(keyword);
			}
		});

		$("#search-undergraduate-certs").on("click", function() {
			var keyword = $("#undergraduate-certs-search").val();
			if (degreeSearchBaseUrl && keyword) {
				document.location.href = degreeSearchBaseUrl + "/minors/major-list/keyword/" + encodeURIComponent(keyword);
			}
		});

		$("#search-grad").on("click", function() {
			var keyword = $("#grad-search").val();
			if (degreeSearchBaseUrl && keyword) {
				document.location.href = degreeSearchBaseUrl + "/masters-phd/major-list/keyword/" + encodeURIComponent(keyword);
			}
		});

		$(".program-search").keypress(function(event) {
		    if (event.keyCode == 13 || event.which == 13) {
		    	var keyword = $(this).val();
		    	var programType = $(this).data("program-type");
				if (degreeSearchBaseUrl && keyword) {
					document.location.href = degreeSearchBaseUrl + "/" + programType + "/major-list/keyword/" + encodeURIComponent(keyword);
				}
		    }
		});
	});
</script>
	</div>

</div>

<script type="text/javascript">
if ($("#my-programs-tabs").length) {
	$("#my-programs-tabs").css("display", "none");
}

$(document).ready(function() {
	if ($("#my-programs-tabs").length) {
		var startTab = 0;
		
		var defaultTab = $("#default-my-programs-box-tab").val();
		
		if (defaultTab != null && defaultTab != undefined && defaultTab != "") {
			startTab = defaultTab;
		}
		
		$("#my-programs-tabs").css("display", "");
		
		initializeTablist("my-programs-box");
		
		manualActiveTab(document.getElementById("myprograms-link-" + startTab), false);
		
		changeProgramsTab(parseInt(startTab));
		
		addLinkTracking($("#my-programs-tabs"));
	}

	$("#anticipated-grad-term-banner-dismiss").click(function() {
		$("#anticipated-grad-term-banner").hide();

		var token = $('#my-programs-user-form-token').val();
		if (token !== undefined) {
			var ajaxData = {
				token: token,
				func: "alert-message-dismiss",
				alert: "ANTICIPATED_GRAD_TERM_BANNER",
				custom: $('#aa-grad-term-cyyt').val(),
			};

			$.ajax({
				cache: false,
				url: "pref",
				type: "POST",
				data: ajaxData,
				error: function() {
					//console.log('Error storing system message dismissal!');
				}
			});
		}
	});

	$("#candidacy-advance-congrats-dismiss").click(function() {
		$("#candidacy-advance-congrats-container").addClass("candidacy-advance-congrats-container-dismissed");
		$("#candidacy-advance-congrats-icon-container").remove();
		$(this).remove();

		var planCollegeAcadPlan = $(this).data("plancollege-acad-plan");

		var token = $('#my-programs-user-form-token').val();
		if (token !== undefined) {
			var ajaxData = {
				token: token,
				func: "add-new-value-to-pref-list",
				set: "MY_PROGRAMS_CANDIDACY_ADVANCE_CONGRATS_BANNER",
				value: planCollegeAcadPlan,
			};

			$.ajax({
				cache: false,
				url: "pref",
				type: "POST",
				data: ajaxData,
				error: function() {
					//console.log('Error storing system message dismissal!');
				}
			});
		}
	});

	$(".milestone-congrats-dismiss").click(function() {
		var milestone = $(this).data("exam-milestone");
		
		$("#milestone-congrats-container-" + milestone).remove();

		var planCollegeAcadPlan = $(this).data("plancollege-acad-plan");

		var token = $('#my-programs-user-form-token').val();
		if (token !== undefined) {
			var ajaxData = {
				token: token,
				func: "add-new-value-to-pref-list",
				set: "MY_PROGRAMS_MILESTONE_CONGRATS_BANNER",
				value: planCollegeAcadPlan,
				subset: milestone,
			};

			$.ajax({
				cache: false,
				url: "pref",
				type: "POST",
				data: ajaxData,
				error: function() {
					//console.log('Error storing system message dismissal!');
				}
			});
		}
	});
});

function changeProgramsTab(idx) {
	if (cluetipInitted["prg"+idx] == null) {
		cluetipInitted["prg"+idx] = 1;

		var relm = $("#my-programs-tabs div.tab-page:eq("+idx+")");

		$('a.cluetip', relm).cluetip("destroy");
		$('a.cluetip', relm).cluetip({activation: 'click', width: 230, showTitle: false,
			sticky: true, closePosition: 'bottom', closeText: CLUETIP_CLOSE,
			arrows: true, local: true});

		$('a.cluetip-title', relm).cluetip("destroy");
		$('a.cluetip-title', relm).cluetip({activation: 'click', width: 230, showTitle: true,
			sticky: true, closePosition: 'title', closeText: CLUETIP_CLOSE,
			arrows: true, local: true, onShow: function(ct, c) {
				addLinkTracking(c);
			}});

		$('a.cluetipWide', relm).cluetip("destroy");
		$('a.cluetipWide', relm).cluetip({activation: 'click', width: 320, showTitle: false,
			sticky: true, closePosition: 'bottom', closeText: CLUETIP_CLOSE,
			arrows: true, local: true});

		$('a.cluetipTitle', relm).cluetip("destroy");
		$('a.cluetipTitle', relm).cluetip({activation: 'click', width: 230, showTitle: true,
			sticky: true, closePosition: 'title', closeText: CLUETIP_CLOSE,
			arrows: true, local: true});

		$('a.gradHover', relm).cluetip("destroy");
		$('a.gradHover', relm).cluetip({activation: 'click', width: 320, showTitle: false,
			sticky: false, closePosition: 'bottom', closeText: CLUETIP_CLOSE,
			arrows: true, local: true, hoverIntent: {sensitivity:  2, interval: 200}
		});
	}
}

</script></div>

				<button role="tab" aria-selected="true" aria-controls="events_tab" id="events_link" data-tab-scope="cal_content" onclick="return changeFeedSection('events', 'cal_content', 0, this);" class="box-tab-selected" fdprocessedid="5p60sp">ASU Events</button>

<script>
	var feedCache = [];
	var forceCalClose = false;
	var ajaxFeedHandlers = [];

	function setupFACalendarHover(){//this doesn't matter so much because this box is going to have a new style of showing content.
		$('.finances-calendar-hover').cluetip({activation: 'click', width: 240, showTitle: false,
			sticky: false, cluezIndex: 105, closeText: CLUETIP_CLOSE, arrows: true, local: true, 
			hideLocal: true, hoverIntent: {sensitivity:  2, interval: 200},
			onShow: function() {
				trackEvent("FA Calender Expl Hover");
			}
		});
	}

	function changeFeedSection(section, update, start, linkElem, feedURL, ajaxUpdate) {
		if (typeof linkElem !== "undefined" && linkElem !== null) {
			var link = $(linkElem);
			link.siblings('a.selected').removeClass("selected");
			link.parent().siblings().children('a.selected').removeClass("selected");
			link.addClass("selected");
		}
		if (typeof ajaxUpdate === "undefined" || ajaxUpdate === null) {
			ajaxUpdate = true;
		}
		if (ajaxUpdate && $("#"+update+":hidden").length > 0) {
			myASUToggle(update.substring(0, update.indexOf("_")));
		}
		if (update == 'cal_content') {
			if (typeof eventcarousel_resize != "undefined" && eventcarousel_resize != null) {
				$(window).unbind('resize', eventcarousel_resize);
				eventcarousel_resize = null;
			}
			if (typeof eventcarousel_internalresize != "undefined" && eventcarousel_internalresize != null) {
				$(window).unbind('resize', eventcarousel_internalresize);
				eventcarousel_internalresize = null;
			}
		}
		$("#"+update).html("<p class='textcenter loading'><img src='images/loader_all_yellow.gif' alt='Loading your data...'/></p>");
		var url = "feed?num=4&feed="+section;
		if (typeof feedURL !== "undefined" && feedURL !== null && feedURL.length != 0) {
			url += "&url="+escape(feedURL);
		}
		url += "&start="+start;

		
			url += "&src=student";
		

		

		// abort if a handler already exists
		if (ajaxFeedHandlers[update] != null) {
			ajaxFeedHandlers[update].abort();
			ajaxFeedHandlers[update] = null;
		}
		
		var viewMoreLink = "<div id='view_more_"+section+"'><p class='view-more'><a href='#' onclick=\"changeFeedSection('"+section+"', 'view_more_"+section+"', "+(start+4)+", null, '"+feedURL+"', "+ajaxUpdate+"); return false;\">View More</a></p></div>";
		if (feedCache[url]) {
			$update = $("#"+update);
			$update.html(feedCache[url]);
			
			$('a', $update).each(function() {
				$(this).click(function() {
					trackEvent("Link", update+"/"+section+"/article");
				});
			});

			$('.story, .story_cal', $update).cluetip({activation: 'click', width: 400, showTitle: false,
				sticky: false, closePosition: 'top', closeText: CLUETIP_CLOSE,
				arrows: true, local: true, hoverIntent: {sensitivity:  2, interval: 200}, 
				clickThrough: true, onShow: function() {
					trackEvent("Popup", update+"/"+section+"/description");
				}
			});

			if (section == 'finances-fa-merged') {
				setupFACalendarHover();
			}
		} else {
			ajaxFeedHandlers[update] = $.ajax({
				type: 'GET',
				url: url,
				dataType: 'html',
				success: function(responseText, textStatus) {
					if (responseText == "") {
						this.error();
						return;
					}
					feedCache[url] = responseText;

					$update = $("#"+update);
					$update.html(responseText);

					$('a', $update).each(function() {
						$(this).click(function() {
							trackEvent("Link", update+"/"+section+"/article");
						});
					});

					$('.story, .story_cal', $update).cluetip({activation: 'click', width: 400, showTitle: true, escapeTitle: true,
						sticky: false, closePosition: 'top', closeText: CLUETIP_CLOSE, /*fx: {open: 'fadeIn', openSpeed: 'fast'},*/
						arrows: true, local: true, hoverIntent: {sensitivity:  2, interval: 200}, 
						clickThrough: true, onShow: function() {
							trackEvent("Popup", update+"/"+section+"/description");
						}
					});

					if (section == 'finances-fa-merged') {
						setupFACalendarHover();
					}
				},
				error: function (XMLHttpRequest, textStatus, errorThrown) {
					$("#"+update).html("<p class='textcenter'>An error occurred while loading this feed.</p>");
				}				
			});
		}
		if (ajaxUpdate && update == 'cal_content') {
			updateUserPref('RSS_SELECTED_'+update, section, null, true);
		}
		if (ajaxUpdate) {
			trackEvent("Toggle", update+"/"+section);
		}
		return false;
	}
	function updateFeedDisplay(section, value, ajaxUpdate) {
		if (typeof ajaxUpdate === "undefined" || ajaxUpdate == null) {
			ajaxUpdate = true;
		}
		if (!value) { // remove section
			$("#"+section+"_link").css("display", "none");
			if ($("#"+section+"_link a").hasClass("selected")) {
				$("#"+section+"_link").parent().children("span:visible").eq(0).children("a").click();
			}
		} else { // add section
			$("#"+section+"_link").css("display", "");
		}

		// update tablist indexes
		initializeTablist("cal_content");
		initializeTablist("news_content");

		// Update all other boxes
		$("."+section+"_edit input[type=checkbox]").each(function() {
			if (value) {
				this.setAttribute("checked", "checked");
			} else {
				$(this).removeAttr("checked");
			}
		});
		if (ajaxUpdate) {
			updateUserPref('updateRss', 'updateDisplay', {key: section, display: value?"show":"hide"});
		}
	}

	$(document).ready(function() {
		//changeFeedSection(section, update, start, linkElem, feedURL, ajaxUpdate)
		// why is this here and not in the news box code?
		changeFeedSection('news_announce', 'news_content', 0, null, null, false);
		
		var usersCal = 'events';
		changeFeedSection(usersCal, 'cal_content', 0, null, null, false);

		$('.edittip a').unbind('click.cluetip'); //avoid multiple click bindings resulting in double-toggle
		$('.edittip a').cluetip({activation: 'click', width: 260, showTitle: false,
			sticky: true, closePosition: 'top', closeText: CLUETIP_CLOSE,
			arrows: true, local: true});

		initializeTablist("cal_content");

		manualActiveTab(document.getElementById("events_link"), false);
	});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	var customID = 0;
	function addFeed() {
		var url = "";
		var possible_urls = $(".news_add_url");
		for (var i = 0; i < possible_urls.length; i++) {
			var temp = $(possible_urls[i]).val();
			if (temp.length != 0) {
				url = temp;
			}
		}
		var name = "";
		var possible_names = $(".news_add_name");
		for (var i = 0; i < possible_names.length; i++) {
			var temp = $(possible_names[i]).val();
			if (temp.length != 0) {
				name = temp;
			}
		}
		if (url.length == 0) {
			alert ("Please enter a RSS feed URL.");
			return;
		}
		if (url.indexOf('feed://') == 0) {
			url = 'http://'+url.substring(7);
		}
		if (!urlValid(url)) {
			alert("The URL you entered is not valid.");
			return;
		}
		// now check the name
		// remove any html characters
		name.replace(/<\/?[^>]+(>|$)/g, "");
		if (name.length == 0) {
			alert ("Please name the new feed.");
			return;
		}
		
		$(".custom_feeds").each(function(i) {
			var newHTML = '<p class="clr news_custom_'+customID+'_edit">';
			newHTML += '<span class="floatleft"><input type="checkbox" value="news_custom_'+customID+'"  class="news_custom_'+customID+'_checkbox"  onclick="updateFeedDisplay(this.value, this.checked)"/><label for="news_custom_'+customID+'">'+name+'</label></span>';
			newHTML += '<span class="floatright"><a href="#remove" onclick="removeFeed(\'news_custom_'+customID+'\');return false;" class="nounderline"><img src="images/delete2.gif" alt="Delete" class="vertmiddle"/></a></span>';
			newHTML += '</p>';
			$(this).append(newHTML);
		});
		$("#news_content_tablist").append('<button role="tab" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="news_custom_' + customID + '_tab" id="news_custom_' + customID + '_link" data-tab-scope="news_content" style="display:none" onclick="return changeFeedSection(\'news_custom\', \'news_content\', 0, this, \''+url+'\');" tabindex="-1">' + name + '</button>');
		// Empty out fields
		$(".news_add_url").each(function() {
			$(this).val("");
		});
		$(".news_add_name").each(function() {
			$(this).val("");
		});
		// Lets send the ajax call to save
		updateUserPref('updateRss', 'addFeed', {key: 'news_custom_'+customID, url: url, name: name});
		customID++;

		trackEvent("Link", "news_content/addFeed");
	}
	function removeFeed(id) {
		// First, make sure it is unchecked
		updateFeedDisplay(id, false, false);
		// Then remove it from the popup
		$("."+id+"_edit").each(function() {
			$(this).remove();
		});
		// Then remove it from the title bar
		$("#"+id+"_link").remove();

		updateUserPref('updateRss', 'removeFeed', {key: id});
	}
	
	$('#edit').unbind('click.cluetip');
	$('#edit').cluetip({activation: 'click', width: 260, showTitle: false,
		sticky: true, closePosition: 'top', closeText: CLUETIP_CLOSE,
		arrows: true, local: true});
	
	initializeTablist("news_content");
</script>
